本轮收口说明(2026-05-14,2026-05-16续修,2026-05-17复核):本表是从 &#39;architecture-design-review.md&#39; 多轮 review 自动抽取得到的累计问题表,存在大量跨轮重复项。 In this round, the final rounds A–G and the tail entries 741–783 serve as the primary focus for wrapping up code, configuration, UI, documentation, and testing; historical duplicates are consolidated into a single fix record. Following the review on 2026-05-17, the two “large-scale testing governance items” (703/726) previously listed in the table will no longer be retained as “open defects.” Instead, they have been reclassified, consistent with their original nature as outlined in Section 2.3 of ‘architecture-design-review.md,’ as “Reviewed (Governance Observations):” the current exact count will be preserved, and the rationale for not making changes will remain unchanged; however, repository‑scale observations will not be misrepresented as one‑time code defects.

&gt; Secondary review boundary (supplementary verification on May 14–17, 2026): This round addresses only the documentation issues listed in this table and the minor warehouse‑level defects referenced within it; no new items outside the table will be added. Large‑scale structural items (such as splitting monolithic files, managing script and directory counts, governing the number of global mocks, anys, and TODOs, and ensuring long‑term synchronization of cross‑language documentation) have already been handled as “governance items” and will no longer be falsely marked as fully refactored using templated “fixed” evidence. On 2026-05-17, a full‑scale test was conducted for the current warehouse, and the results have been included as evidence in this table.

&gt; 3rd review and reconstruction (2026-05-14): First, the original templated columns “Review Conclusion,” “Root Cause Classification,” and “Evidence” in 783 rows were cleared; then, based on the region, issue, file path, and recommended fix for each row, they were reclassified and repopulated; after the review, the same rationale is no longer used to batch overwrite all issues.

&gt; 4 authoritative audits (2026-05-16): &#39;node scripts/ci/audit-review-batch-resource-contracts.mjs&#39;, &#39;node scripts/ci/audit-codebase-inventory.mjs&#39;, &#39;node scripts/ci/audit-review-governance-closures.mjs&#39;, and &#39;npm audit --prefix ui&#39; have been re-executed; the current authoritative results are &#39;118/118&#39;, &#39;11/11&#39;, &#39;9/9&#39;, and &#39;found 0 vulnerabilities&#39;, respectively; artifacts in the root directory &#39;:memory:*&#39;, &#39;artifacts/&#39;, and &#39;session-replay/&#39; have been cleaned up. Certain historical entries in the table still retain the interim counts recorded during the phased reviews at the time (e.g., ‘46/46’, ‘69/69’, ‘88/88’, ‘92/92’, ‘96/96’, ‘103/103’). | Plugin Runtime Sandbox and Subprocess Listener | Fixed | The ‘AA_PLUGIN_SANDBOX_ROOT’ environment variable was directly used with ‘chdir’, and the host did not explicitly clean up the child listener/process tracker. | Added sandbox root validation in ‘plugin-runtime-child.ts’; added resource cleanup and workspace environment setup in ‘plugin-runtime-host.ts’; targeted testing of the plugin runtime has passed. |
| DomainLifecycleState duplication/inconsistency | Fixed | The remediation module uses PascalCase states, while domain-specs uses canonical states | ‘src/domains/architecture-remediation.ts’ now uses the ‘domain-specs’ canonical type; ‘domain-specs.ts’ retains the legacy alias for backward compatibility; invariant tests pass |
| SDK Security and Determinism | Fixed | The SBOM remote heuristic can lead to false vulnerability inferences, RSA‑2048 is relatively weak, and test‑ID/mock error injection lacks determinism | Disable the remote heuristic in `plugin-definition.ts`; upgrade to RSA‑4096 in `pack-manifest.ts`; use `randomUUID` in `fixture-redact.ts`; employ a seeded PRNG in `pack-test-local-service.ts`; SDK‑specific tests pass |

| Ops Chaos / Benchmark / TrustLevel | Fixed | The chaos scheduler used &#39;console.*&#39; and raw callbacks with async intervals; the benchmark success baseline was not a percentile; the TrustLevel enumeration had duplicates. | In &#39;chaos-experiment-scheduler.ts&#39;, &#39;StructuredLogger&#39; was used along with try/catch for the interval; in &#39;benchmark-runner.ts&#39;, a weighted percentile was added; in &#39;trust-level.ts&#39;, the enumeration was unified; and the corresponding targeted tests passed. |

| Test Skips/Cross‑Border Pipeline/Budget Integration | Fixed | ‘budget-allocation.integration.test.ts’ still uses ‘test.skip()’ to bypass multi‑dimensional quota and workflow_state setup; ‘cross‑region-routing.test.ts’ employs ‘describe.skip()’ to skip the five‑step cross‑border pipeline; the comprehensive tests still retain the “not yet implemented” legacy assertions. | ‘evaluateMultiDimensionalQuota()’ has been integrated into the budget tests, and the reservation/settlement tests now fully account for ‘workflow_state’ and step outputs; the ‘CrossRegionRoutingService’ has added a five‑step pipeline covering jurisdiction, impact, mechanism, minimization, and output scanning; the associated 47 targeted tests have passed with skipped=0.
| Queue/Tail‑of‑Table Failure Test/Dependency Audit | Verified | The retry, purge, and stats semantics of the SQLite/Redis queue adapters are susceptible to being overridden by in‑memory mocks or masked by spurious counter drift; the targeted tests at lines 773–776 need revalidation; issue 783 requires current audit evidence. | The SQLite queue maintains the database as the single source of truth: `purge()` removes only completed or dead‑letter jobs older than the cutoff; Redis’s `retryJobAsync()` applies only to failed or dead‑letter jobs, and `statsAsync()` falls back to Redis set counts. A total of 130 queue‑ and domain‑specific tests passed, along with 38 targeted tests at lines 773–776, and `npm audit` reported “found 0 vulnerabilities.” |
| Recovery / Plugin executor / Side effect | Fixed | The recovery decision path previously read the `execution` outside of a transaction, and the `latestCheckpoint` summary read was overridden by a no-op implementation; the plugin executor would swallow validation errors as ordinary results; the side‑effect escalation’s state mapping was inaccurate. | In `runtime-recovery-decision-service*.ts`, the `execution` is re-read within the transaction and the same snapshot is passed to the event log; in `runtime-recovery-service.ts`, checkpoint artifact reading has been restored; in `adapter/browser/human/sub-workflow executor`, `ValidationError` is explicitly preserved along with the run ID; in `side-effect-manager.ts`, a state machine–based approach is adopted, and HITL escalation is mapped to ambiguous.
| Document/Structure‑Related Historical Duplicates | Merged | Multiple rounds of review have repeatedly documented the same issues—such as “excessive large files/scripts/directories” and “document synchronization.” | This round adds ‘docs_zh/reference/api-client.md,’ corrects the UI README path, and marks ‘src/core’ as legacy; major structural evolutions like splitting monolithic files are not presented as one‑off completions but are deferred to subsequent architecture governance and will no longer block the current round’s closed‑loop defect resolution.
